Question: What is 'roll back' in database terms?
A. Reverting a transaction to its previous state
B. Applying a saved database dump
C. Rolling the data on screen
D. None of the above
Answer: A

Level: A-Level
Topic: Security
Question: What is symmetric key encryption?
A. Encryption where the same key is used for encryption and decryption
B. Encryption where one key encrypts and a different key decrypts
C. A key with equal length on both sides
D. Encryption only for symmetric networks
Answer: A

Level: A-Level
Topic: Security
Question: What is asymmetric key encryption?
A. Encryption that uses a public key and a private key for encryption and decryption
B. Encryption where both keys are the same
C. Encryption that uses no keys
D. Encryption only for secure networks
Answer: A
